<div class="table_fields_question" style="width:150px;">Limit Display: <img border="0" onmouseout="UnTip()" onmouseover="TagToTip('CookiesText')" src="images/question.gif"/>
<span id="CookiesText" style="display:none;">
<b>CANCELED Appointments</b> are appointments which have been deleted from the schedule.
<br/><br/>
<b>CLIENT REPORT FORMS</b> are post-session forms entered after an appointment has concluded.  Limiting the report to client report forms also displays off-schedule client report forms.
<br/><br/>
<b>eTUTORING APPOINTMENTS</b> are appointments for which "eTutoring" has been selected when the appointment was made.
<br/><br/>
<b>NO-SHOW Appointments</b> are appointments that have the "missed" or "no-show" checkbox selected.
<br/><br/>
<b>ONLINE Appointments</b> are appointments for which the WCONLINE Online Consulting Module is being used.
<br/><br/>
<b>ORPHAN Appointments</b> are appointments for which no post-session client report form has been entered.
<br/><br/>
<b>PLACEHOLDER Appointments</b> are appointments that have the "placeholder" checkbox selected.
<br/><br/>
<b>WALK-IN Appointments</b> are appointments that have the "walk-in" or "drop-in" checkbox selected.
</span></div>

$(document).ready(function() {
    var triggers = $(".modalInput").overlay({
      fixed: false,
      mask: {
        color: '#CCCCCC',
        loadSpeed: 200,
        opacity: 0.8
      },
      closeOnClick: false
  });
    var buttons = $("#yesno button").click(function(e) {
      var yes = buttons.index(this) === 0;
      triggers.eq(0).html("You clicked " + (yes ? "yes" : "no"));
  });
    $("#prompt form").submit(function(e) {
      triggers.eq(1).overlay().close();
      var input = $("input", this).val();
      triggers.eq(1).html(input);
      return e.preventDefault();
  });
  });
</script>
